                    <p xml:id="SS.1.1.0"><pb n="1v"/><milestone facs="1v" unit="folio"/>namaḥ
                            sar<unclear reason="damaged">vvabuddha</unclear>bodhisatvebhyaḥ|| namo
                            nāgārju<unclear>na</unclear>pādāya|| </p>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.1">athāto vedotpattim ādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.2"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.3">atha khalu bhagavantam amaravara ṛṣigaṇaparivṛtam
                        āśramasthaṃ kāśirājaṃ divodāsam aupadhenava<pc
                            > </pc>vaistaraṇaurabhra<pc> </pc>pauṣkalāvata<pc
                            > </pc>karavīra<pc> </pc>gopurarakṣita<pc> </pc>bhoja<pc
                            > </pc>suśruta<pc> </pc>prabhṛtavya ūcuḥ|| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.4">bhagavañ charīramānasāgantubhir vyādhibhi vividhavedanā<lb
                            n="2"/>bhighātopadrutān āsanāthān anāthavad viceṣṭamānān vikrośataś ca
                        mānavān abhisamīkṣya manasi naḥ pīḍābhavat || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.4b"> teṣāṃ sukhaiṣiṇāṃ rogopagamārtham ātmanaś ca
                        prāṇayātārtham āyurvedaṃ icchāmaḥ | upadiśyamānam atrāyattam aihikam
                        āmuṣmikañ ca śreyas tad bhagavantam upasannā sma | śiṣyatveneti</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.5">tān uvāca bhagavān svāgatam vaḥ sava evāmīmāṃsyā a<lb n="3"
                        />dhyāpyāś ca bhavanto vatsāḥ||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.6">iha khalv āyurvedo nāma yad upāgam atharvavedasyoktam
                        anutpādyaiva ca prajāḥ ślokaśatasahasram adhyāyasahasrañ ca kṛtavān
                        svayambhūr alpāyuṣkālpamedhastvañ cālokya narāṇāṃ bhūyo ṣṭadhā
                        praṇītavān</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.7">tad yathā | śalyaṃ śālākyaṃ
                        kāyacikitsābhūtavidyākaumārabhṛtyam agadatantraṃ rasāyanatantraṃ
                        vājīkaraṇatantram iti| </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.1">athāsya pra<lb n="4"/>ty<unclear reason="damaged"
                            >e</unclear>kāṅgalakṣaṇasamāsas </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.1a">tatra śaṃlyan nāma
                            vividhatṛṇakāṣṭhapāṣāṇapāṃsulohalo<unclear reason="illegible"
                            >ṣṭā</unclear>sthibālanapūyāsrāva<unclear reason="damaged"
                            >du</unclear><gap quantity="2" reason="damaged" unit="akṣara"
                            /><unclear>ṇā</unclear>n<gap quantity="1" reason="damaged" unit="akṣara"
                        />rgarbhaśalyoddharaṇārthaṃ yantraśastrakṣārāgnipraṇidhānaviniścayārthañ ca
                        ṣaṣṭyābhidhānair iti |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.2">śālākyatantran nāmordhvajatrugatānāṃ vikārāṇā
                        śravaṇanayanavadanaghrāṇādisaṃśritānā vikārāṇām upaśamakaraṇārtham </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.3">kā<lb n="5"/>yacikītsā nāma sarvaśarīrāvasthitānāñ ca
                        vyādhīnām upaśamakaraṇārthaṃ
                        jvaraśophagulmaraktapittonmādāpasmārapramehātīsārādīnāñ ca |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.4">bhūtavidyā nāma
                        devadīnavagandharvayakṣarākṣasapitṛpiśācavināyakanāgagrahopasṛṣṭacetasāṃ
                        śāntikarmabaliharaṇādigrahopaśamanārtham |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.5">kaumārabhṛtyan nāma kumārabharaṇadhātrīkṣīrado<lb n="6"
                        />ṣasaṃśodhanārtham duṣṭastanyagrahasamutthitānāñ ca vyādhīnām
                        upaśamakaraṇārthaḥ |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.6"> agadatantran nāma
                        sarpakīṭalūtādaṣṭasarīsṛpaviṣavyañjanārtha vividhaviṣavegopaśamanārthañ ca
                        ||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.7"> rasāyanatantran nāma vayasthāpanam āyurmedhākaraṇaṃ
                        vyādhyupaśamakaraṇārthañ ca |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.8"> vājīkaraṇatantran nāma svalpaduṣṭakṣīṇaviśuṣkaretasāṃ
                            śukrāpyāya<lb n="7"/>naprasādopacayajanananimittaṃ praharṣajananārthañ
                        ca |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.9"> evam ayam āyurvedo ṣṭāṅga upadiśyate | atra kasmai kim
                        varṇyatām iti |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.10">ta ūcuḥ | asmākaṃ sarveṣām eva na<subst>
                            <del rend="cancelled">nam eva</del>
                        </subst> śalyajñānam alaṅ kṛtvopadiśatu <unclear reason="illegible"
                            >bha</unclear>gavān iti | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.11"> sa uvāca evaṃm astv iti</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.12"> ta ūcuḥ | bhūyo 'smāka sarveṣāṃm evaikamatīnānām matam
                        abhisamīkṣya suśruto bhagavantaṃ pra<pb n="2r"/><milestone facs="2r"
                            unit="folio"/>tyakṣasyopadiśyamānaṃ vayam apy upadhārayiṣyāmaḥ |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.13">sa uvācaivam astv iti | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.14-16"> iha khalv āyuvedaprayojanaṃ vyādhyupasṛṣṭasya
                        vyādhiparimokṣaḥ | svastharakṣaṇañ cāyur asmin vidanty anena vāyu vidyata
                        ity āyurvedas tasyāṅgavaram āgamapratyakṣānumānopamānair aviruddham
                        ucyamānam upadhārayadhvam </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.17"> etad dhy aṅgaṃ prathamaṃ pradhānaṃ prāgabhidhānatvād
                        vraṇasaṃrohaṇakaratvād yajña<lb n="2"/>śirapradhānasandhānāc ca śrūyate hi
                        yathā purā rudreṇa yajñasya śiraś chinnam aśvi<unclear reason="smudged"
                            >bhyā</unclear>ṃ punaḥ sandhitam iti </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.18"> aṣṭānām api cāyurvedatantrāṇām etad evādhikam
                        āśukriyākaraṇād yantraśastrakṣārāgnipraṇidhānāt sarvatantrasāmānyāc ca |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.19"> tad ida śāśvata puṇyaṃ svargyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ
                        vṛttikarañ ca | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.20"> ta brahmā provāca | tat prajāpatir
                            adhija<unclear>ce</unclear> | tasmād aśvināv aśvibhyām indra<lb n="3"/>
                        indrād ahaṃ mayā tv iha pradeyam arthibhyaḥ prajāhitahetoḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.20x">bha |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.21"> ahaṃ hi dhanvantarir ādidevo jarārujāmṛtyuharo marāṇāṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śalyam mahacchastravaraṃ gṛhītvā prāpto mi gāṃ bhūya ihopadeṣṭuṃ | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.22"> tatrāsmiñ chāstre pañcamahābhūtaśarīrisama<unclear
                            reason="eccentric_ductus">v</unclear>āyaḥ puruṣa ity ucyate | tasmiṃ
                        kriyā so dhiṣṭhānaṃ kasmāl laukikavidhyāl loko hi dvividhasthāvarajaṅgamaś
                        ca dvividhātmaka e<lb n="4"/>vāgneyaḥ | saumyaś ca tadbhūyastvāt pañcātako
                        vā | tatra caturvidho bhūtagrāmaḥ | saṃsvedajādridajajarāyujāṇḍajasaṃ<gap
                            quantity="1" reason="damaged" unit="akṣara" extent="sūtra hole jñā"/>s
                        tasmiṃ puruṣaḥ pradhānas tasyopakaraṇam anyaṃ tasmāt puruṣo dhiṣṭhānaṃ </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.23"> tadduḥkhasaṃyogā vyādhaya ity ucyante | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.24"> te caturvidhā āgantavaḥ śārīrā mānasā svābhāvikāś ceti
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.1"> teṣv āgantavo bhighātanimittā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.2"> śārīrās tv annamūlā vātapittakapha<lb n="5"
                        />śoṇitavaiṣamyanimittāḥ </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.3"> mānasās tu
                        krodhaśokadainyaharṣakāmaviṣāderṣyāsūyāmātsaryalobhādaya icchādveṣanimittāḥ| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.4"> svābhāvikās tu kṣutpipāsājarāmṛtyunidrāprabhṛtayaḥ </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.26"> ete manaḥśarīrādhiṣṭhānā bhavanti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.27"> teṣāṃ lekhanabṛ<unclear>mha</unclear>na
                        saṃśodhanasaṃśamanāhārācārāḥ samyakprayuktā nigrahahetavo bhavanti |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.28"> prāṇināṃ puna mūlam ā<lb n="6"/>hāro balavarṇṇaujasāñ ca
                        sa ṣaṭsu raseṣv āyattarasāḥ punar davyāśrayinā dravyāṇi punar oṣadhyaḥ | tā
                        dvividhā | sthāvarā jaṅgamāś ca | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.29"> tāsāṃ sthāvarāś caturvidhā | vanaspatayo vṛkṣā auṣadhyo
                        vīrudha iti | tāsv apuṣpā <gap quantity="1" unit="akṣara" extent="gap in the
                            writing with a cross"/>lavantyo vanaspatayaḥ | puṣpaphalo yye tā vṛkṣāḥ
                        | phalapākaniṣṭhās tv auṣadhyaḥ | pratānavantyo virudha iti ||<lb n="7"
                        /></l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.30"> jaṅgamā khalv api caturvvidhā |
                        jarāyujāṇḍajasasvedajodbhidāḥ iti | teṣām paśumanuṣyavyālādayo jarāyujāḥ |
                        khagasarīsṛpasarpās tv aṇḍajāḥ | kṛmikuṭṭhapipīlikāprabhṛtayaḥ saṃsvedajāḥ |
                        indragopakamaṇḍūkaprabhṛtayaś codbhidāḥ | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.31"> tatra sthāvarebhyas
                        tvakpatrapuṣpaphalamūlakandakṣīraniryāsasārasnehasvarasā prayojanavantaḥ<pb
                            n="2v"/><milestone facs="2v" unit="folio"/> jaṅgamebhyaś
                        carmaromanakharudhirādayaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.32"> pārthivas tu suvarṇṇarajatādayaḥ | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.33"> kālakṛtās tu
                        pravātanivātātapacchāyātamojyotsnāśītoṣṇavarṣāsu sasamplavāḥ | kālaviśeṣās
                        tu nimeṣakāṣṭhākalāmuhūrttāhorātrapakṣamāsartvayanasamvatsarayugaviśeṣāḥ | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.34"> svabhāvata eva doṣāṇāṃ sañcayaprakopaśamapratīkārahetavo
                        bhavanti |<lb n="2"/> prayojanavantaś ca || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.35"> bha || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.35x"> śārīrāṇāṃ vikārāṇām eṣa vargeś caturvvidhaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prakope praśame caiva hetur ukta cikitsakaiḥ | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.36"> āgantavas tu ye rogās te dvidhā nipatanti ha |
                        <caesura/>
                         manasy anye śarīre ca teṣān tu dvividhā kriyā || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.37"> śarīrapatitānān tu śārīravadupakramaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mānasānān tu śabdādir iṣṭo vargaḥ sukhāvahaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.38"> evam etat puru<lb n="3"/>ṣo vyādhir auṣadhaṃ kriyākāla
                        iti samāsena catuṣṭayaṃ vyākhyātam bhavati || tatra puruṣagrahaṇāt
                        tatsambhavadravyasamūho bhūtādir uktaḥ | tadagadgapratyaṅgavikalpāś ca |
                        tvaṅmāṃsāsirāsnāyvasthisandhiprabhṛtayaḥ | vyādhigrāhaṇād
                        vātapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātāgantusvabhāvanimittāḥ | sarvva eva vyādhayo
                            vyākhyā<lb n="4"/>tā bhavasvanti | oṣadhagrahaṇād
                        dravyarasaguṇavīryavipākānām ādeśaḥ | kriyāgrahaṇāt | snehādīni cchedyādīni
                        ca karmāṇy upadiṣṭāni bhavanti | kālagrahaṇāt sarvva eva kriyākālanirdeśaḥ
                        || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.39x"> bha </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.39"> bījaṃ cikitsitasyaitat samāsena prakīrttitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.1"> athāto hitīhitīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.3"> yad vāyoḥ pathyaṃ tat pittasyāpathyam iti anena hetunā na
                            kiñci<cb n="3"/>d dravyam ekāntena hitam ahitam vāstīti kecid ācārya
                        bruvate || taṃ tu na samyak | iha khalu dravyāṇi svabhāvataḥ | <lb n="5"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.1"> athātaḥ cchāyāvipratipattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.4ab"> hrīr apakrāmati yataḥ kā<lb n="3"/><unclear

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.5ab"> yasyādharauṣṭhaṃ patitaḥ kṣiptaś corddhan tatho<cb
                            n="1"/>ttaraḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.5cd"> ubhau vā jāmbavābhāsau sa parāsur asaṃśayam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.6ab"> ā raktā daśanā yasya syāvā va syuḥ patanti vā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.6cd"> khāñjanapratibhā vā<cb n="2"/>pi taṅ gatāyuṣam ādiśet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.7ab"> kṛṣṇā snigdhāvaliptā jihvā gunā ca yasya vai | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.7cd"> karkaśā ca bhaved yasya so <lb n="4"/>cirād vijahāty
                        asūn | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.8ab"> kuṭilā sphuṭitā vāpi śūnā vā yasya nāsikā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.8cd"> bhagnā vā sphurate vāpi sa pa<cb n="1"/>rāsur asaṃsayaḥ
                        | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.9ab"> saṃkṣipte viṣame stabdhe rakte supte ca locane | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.9cd"> yasya syātāṃ śrute vāpi sa parāsu asaṃśayaṃ | </l>

                        āsyagaṃ | </l>

                        | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.13cd"> viprasāraṇaśīlo vā sa parāsur asaṃśayaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.1"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.1.1"> dhanvantarimahāprajñaṃ sarvaśāstraviśāradam | caraṇāv

                            n="2"/> māsena kaṣāyo vargaḥ |</l>

                        ca |

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.221">śūlagulmoda<cb n="2"/>rānāhavirekāsthāpanādiṣu
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtraprayogasādhye tu gavyam mūtraṃ payojayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.222">ānāhasophagulmeṣu pāṇḍuro<lb n="5"/>ge tu māhiṣaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śophaghnaṃ mājamaurabhraṃ kāsasvāsavisāpahaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.223"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.224"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.225">āsvaṃ kaphaharaṃ mūtrakrimidardruṣu sasyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.226">tīkṣṇaṃ kṣā<cb n="1"/>re kilāse ca nāgamūtram prayojayet
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.227"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.228">aśoghnaṃ kārabhaṃ mūtraṃ mānuṣan tu viṣāpahaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.229">dravadravyāṇi sarvāṇi kīrttitāni samāsataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         deśakā<cb n="2"/>lavibhāgajño nṛpateḥ karttum arhatīti ||</l>
